It's Similar to famous game Yhatzee / Yatzy / yahtzee.\r\n\r\nIt has well established rules and has a variation in scoring and in play as well.\r\nWell, you gotta play to win and you can't win if you don't play Farkle!\r\n\r\nFarkle is commonly played with a dice, sheet of paper for scoring and a pen/pencil.\r\n\r\nIt is played by two or more players, with each player in succession having a turn at throwing the dice, the players turn results into a score, and after 10 rounds the player reaching 10000 is the winner.\r\n\r\nAt the start of each turn, the player throws the dice(6) all at once. One or more scoring dice will be set aside after each throw. After this the player may then either end their turn and bank the score, or continue to throw the remaining Dice.\r\nIf all six dice are scored, they have a 'hot dice' and continue their turn with a new throw of all the six dice adding to the score they have already accumulated.
